Ping City Suppresses Rising Copper Coin Prices; Jinan Seals Existing Silver and Paper Money 15

(Beiping) The price of copper coins in Ping City continues to skyrocket, and the lives of ordinary people are greatly affected. The Municipal Government has decided to take effective measures to suppress the prices. Grain prices are gradually stabilizing, but there is no downward trend. The Central Bank will transport ten million legal tender to Ping City within days to be exchanged by the three banks (Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Communications) and to redeem banknotes from other banks. (Central News Agency telegram, 13th)

(Jinan) This morning, Han Fuju summoned the Director of the Department of Finance, the Director of the Military Law Department, the Director of the Public Security Bureau, and the Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to the Provincial Government and informed them that the government is determined to seek a livelihood for the majority of the poor. He stated that the prices of grain, rice, and coal have skyrocketed and decided to strictly suppress them. All prices must be restored to the original prices before the 3rd of this month. Violators will have their goods confiscated. Copper coins must also be restored to the original price of twenty-six large coins per dime. He also issued a general order to all county magistrates to check and seal the existing silver in the silver and money houses in each county, prohibiting it from being transported out. In this city, the Department of Finance, the Military Law Department, the Provincial Government, the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and the Public Security Bureau were ordered to check and seal the existing silver in the banks and money houses, with the seals of the Provincial Government and the General Headquarters, prohibiting it from being transported out. Another order stated that the existing silver in this province must be kept within the province. Since the cash is not going out, the market should not be affected in any way. (Special dispatch, 13th)

(Jinan) The Municipal Public Security Bureau sent people to announce along the streets that raising prices is prohibited, and violators will be punished according to law. (Special dispatch, 13th)

(Jinan) The central sub-branch has compiled and reported to the Ministry the number of existing silver and banknotes in the various banks and money houses in Jinan. The silver totals eight million two hundred thousand yuan, and the banknotes total seven million yuan. The existing silver is all sealed for safekeeping and will not be transported out. The Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications telegraphed their respective head offices to transport one-yuan notes to Jinan as much as possible to replace existing currency. (Special dispatch, 13th)

(Bao'an) The implementation of the new legal tender decree is proceeding smoothly. Merchants and civilians have been exchanging at the Central Bank and Bank of Communications in recent days. Because the market has been short of hard currency, the amount exchanged is only several hundred yuan. The Central Bank and Bank of Communications have now transferred a large amount of single-unit legal tender and four types of fractional notes (one dime, two dimes, two dimes and five cents, and five dimes) from the Central Bank of Pingjin for full exchange. Fractional notes from the Central Bank, Bank of China, Bank of Agriculture and Commerce, and Datong that are circulating in the market are still used as usual. The price of copper coins today is 420 to 430 coins. According to people in the financial sector, how the Central Bank and Bank of Communications will dispose of the existing silver will be decided after the establishment of the Tianjin Preparatory Sub-branch. The exchange rate had slightly increased recently due to the listing of cotton in various counties, but it has now stabilized. However, the customs of the people in various counties are conservative, and they do not fully understand the new legal tender decree. The Central Bank and Bank of Communications are now fully prepared for the exchange and can gradually promote the decree. (Central News Agency telegram, 13th)

(Anqing) Recently, due to the implementation of currency policies in Wanyuan (Anqing), the price of copper coins has skyrocketed, and commodity prices have soared. (Wuhu) The financial situation in Wuhu City is very stable recently. League of Nations Sanctions Against Italy; Decision to Implement as Scheduled; Indifference to Italian Protests 22

(Geneva) The Italian government sent protest notes to the governments of various countries participating in sanctions yesterday. Therefore, some parties are deeply afraid that after the economic sanctions are implemented, Italy may retaliate by withdrawing from the League of Nations. However, people in the League of Nations believe that the Italian protest note does not contain the intention of withdrawing from the League of Nations. If the country thinks this move is beneficial, it can do it sooner rather than later. Now that it has been delayed until now, it shows that it does not want to do so. As for the implementation procedure of economic sanctions, since it has been formulated, it will not be changed due to Italian protests and will still be implemented on the original date, that is, November 18. The Adjustment Committee has entrusted Chairman Vasconcelos to monitor the progress of sanctions. If difficulties are encountered, he should solicit opinions from experts from various countries. The eighteen-nation subgroup committee must be convened only when major accidents occur. The League of Nations Secretariat and the Adjustment Committee have not received this Italian protest note. However, Italy denies that the Adjustment Committee is a formal organization of the League of Nations, and this protest note may not be delivered to the committee. (Havas Telegram, 13th)

(London) The British authorities are dealing calmly with the Italian government's note to various countries protesting sanctions and threatening to implement retaliation plans. The public thinks that the statement in the note that Italy's memorandum to the League of Nations has not received appropriate research is contrary to the facts. In addition, the argument held by the Italian government that the Sanctions Adjustment Committee has no foothold is considered by people here to be that Italy does not understand the relationship between member states and the League of Nations. At the same time, people in Geneva think that the note that Italy sent to the member states of the League of Nations is the only way that it can still implement as a member state of the League of Nations. The public feels that the issue of Italy remaining in the League of Nations will be raised soon. When the Fascist Party holds a conference in Rome on November 16, it may propose this matter on its own initiative. (Reuters Telegram, 13th)

(Paris) Those in charge are deeply worried that if the countries continue to implement sanctions against Italy, Italy may retaliate by withdrawing from the League of Nations. Well-informed sources believe that France's reply to Italy will express approval of Italy's wishes. In addition, the general well-informed sources do not believe that the Italian note is enough to cause the various countries participating in sanctions to change their fundamental positions. Austrian Foreign Minister Also Announces Ban on Transporting Military Supplies to Italy; According to the Provisions of the Treaty of Saint-Germain 23

(Vienna) Foreign Minister Walter Neigg declared in the Federal Parliament today that Austria would cooperate with various countries to prohibit the transportation of war materials to Italy. Austria had previously stated in Geneva that it was unwilling to participate in sanctions against Italy. The Foreign Minister's statement today is quite surprising. (Reuters Telegram, 13th)

(Vienna) According to official sources, Austria's attitude towards the sanctions issue is based on the provisions of the Treaty of Saint-Germain, which prohibits Austria from exporting arms to other countries and guarantees that goods from other countries can freely pass through Austria to Italy. In addition, Foreign Minister Weideger recently declared to the press that "Germany is not a member state of the League of Nations, so according to the Treaty of Saint-Germain, Austria cannot prohibit German goods from passing through the territory to Italy." According to a Havas reporter, although Austria and Britain have always had close friendships, Austria had to cancel its pro-active attitude toward sanctions for two reasons. First, Italy saved Austria from being annexed by Germany in 1934. As for the League of Nations, whether it can assist Austria is a question. Seeing that Italian troops have occupied Magale and Golahei, and sanctions against Italy have not yet been implemented, it can be seen that the League of Nations' assistance is slow and does not address the urgent need. Second, the trade between Italy and Austria is beneficial to Austria. Austria relies on the benefits obtained from trade with Italy to pay off foreign debts. Therefore, it cannot participate in sanctions to lose this kind of trade benefit. (Havas Telegram, 13th)

(Vienna) There are rumors that Austria's foreign policy is about to change course. Official circles recently issued a statement stating that this statement is unfounded. Austria's foreign policy has always been based on loyalty to the League of Nations. (Havas Telegram, 13th)

(Vienna) Austrian Chancellor Dr. Schuschnigg stated in the Federal Parliament today that Austria will soon greatly increase its military equipment. Deputy State Chancellor General Zehner also stated that Austria needs more tanks and aircraft. Foreign Minister Walter Neigg explained the basic policy of Austrian diplomacy, especially supporting the principles of the League of Nations, and said that Austria does not take actions to please any country, but only acts for the benefit and trade of its own people. (Reuters Telegram, 12th)

Abyssinian Plant Research: (Moscow, TASS, October 19) The great Soviet scientist Vavilov led a team to Abyssinia in 1927 to investigate local plants. They stayed in Abyssinia for four months, traveling two thousand kilometers and surveying all of the country's major agricultural areas. They collected more than six thousand types of local plants. Vavilov recently published his research results, first stating that Abyssinia is rich in plant species, which are unknown in other countries. Vavilov also stated that although Abyssinia is small and mountainous, the number of wheat species exceeds that of the entire world. As far as botanists know, there are a total of six hundred and fifty types of wheat, and the Abyssinian mountains have two hundred and fifty types. Vavilov continued, stating that Abyssinian plants are very suitable for the Soviet Union. Abyssinian barley is currently being cultivated in the Leningrad Province, Ghibiny beyond the Arctic Circle, and the Kola Peninsula, with good results. The Soviet Union is also using Abyssinian barley and legumes as superior species for hybridization. Abyssinia usually has short days and long nights, so Abyssinian plants can also be cultivated in the Soviet Union's far northern regions during the long days of summer. Among Abyssinian plants, teff grass is now a valuable forage crop in the arid regions of Central Asia.

Educational Broadcast Special

How the Sun, Moon, and Stars Move and the Phenomena Resulting from Their Movement (6) 27

— (Lectures to the national public on October 18, 21, 27, and 28) Researcher at the Institute of Astronomy, Academia Sinica

This classification is based on astronomy, categorized by month for statistical convenience. For instance, if we want the average temperature of spring, we simply calculate the average temperature of March, April, and May. This classification is commonly used in meteorology. As for which of the three classifications is better, there is no set standard; it depends on the climate of each region. From a theoretical perspective, our Chinese classification, the first one, can be said to be the most reasonable. It designates the astronomical time of warmth, the vernal equinox, as the center of spring, and the hottest time, the summer solstice, as the center of summer, which is very appropriate.

Now, we will discuss why the climate of a certain place on Earth has various changes throughout the year. We already know that the Earth's orbit is within the ecliptic plane, and it forms an angle of approximately twenty-three and a half degrees with the Earth's equator. The Earth's axis of rotation is perpendicular to its equator, forming a ninety-degree angle. Therefore, the angle between the Earth's axis of rotation and its orbital plane is also twenty-three and a half degrees, resulting in the Earth's poles having different relationships with the sun at different times. Around July 21st, the Earth's North Pole is tilted twenty-three and a half degrees towards the sun. At this time, the South Pole is in the hemisphere without sunlight, while the North Pole receives sunlight throughout the day. In the Northern Hemisphere, days are long and nights are short; in the Southern Hemisphere, days are short and nights are long. The situation is reversed at the winter solstice, when the South Pole can see the sun all day. During the vernal and autumnal equinoxes, around March 21st and September 23rd, the Earth's equatorial plane passes through the sun, so day and night are equally long everywhere on Earth. Places on the equator have equal day and night lengths throughout the year, so there are virtually no seasons.

The area within twenty-three and a half degrees north and south of the equator is called the tropics, where the sun is overhead throughout the year. The area between twenty-three and a half degrees and sixty-six and a half degrees north and south of the equator is called the temperate zone, where the sun does not pass through the zenith, and the sun is not below the horizon at noon, so the seasonal changes are most pronounced in the temperate zone. China is located within the temperate zone, so the seasonal climate changes are also very significant. The area from the temperate zone to the North and South Poles is called the frigid zone, where the sun is not visible in winter, and in summer, the sun does not set below the horizon but circles around it.

Why is summer hotter than winter in the temperate zone? Some say it's because the Earth is closer to the sun in summer and farther away in winter, but this is incorrect. In the Northern Hemisphere, the Earth is actually closer to the sun in winter than in summer. However, if the Earth is farther away from the sun in summer, why is it hotter than in winter? We know that seasonal climate changes are due to changes in atmospheric temperature, which vary according to the amount of solar heat received by the Earth's surface. The amount of solar heat received by a unit area on the Earth's surface depends on three main factors:

(1) The length of time the sun shines on the ground: the longer the sun shines on the ground, the more solar heat the ground receives.

(2) Whether the sunlight is direct or oblique: the higher the sun's altitude, the more heat the ground receives; the lower the sun's altitude, i.e., oblique sunlight, the less heat the ground receives.

(3) The amount of absorption by the atmosphere: the thicker the path that sunlight passes through the Earth's atmosphere, the more solar heat the atmosphere absorbs, and the less heat the ground receives.

Once we understand the above three relationships, we can understand why summer is hot and winter is cold. We already know that the days are longer in summer, and the sun is closer to the overhead point at noon, meaning the sun's altitude is higher than in winter. The sunlight shines directly on the ground, and it passes through a thinner layer of the atmosphere (the atmosphere is commonly known as air), so the atmosphere absorbs less solar heat, making the weather hot. In winter, the days are shorter, and the sun is farther from the overhead point at noon, meaning the sun's altitude is lower than in summer. The sunlight is oblique, and it passes through a thicker layer of the atmosphere, so the atmosphere absorbs more solar heat, making the weather cold.

Let's start from the vernal equinox, when day and night are equally long. After this, the days gradually become longer than the nights, and the sun's altitude also rises day by day, meaning the sun gradually changes from oblique to direct. Additionally, the layer of atmosphere (the atmosphere is commonly known as air) that sunlight passes through gradually thins, so the weather gradually becomes warmer. By the summer solstice, the days are longest, the sun's altitude is highest, and the sunlight passes through the thinnest layer of the atmosphere, making the weather the hottest. After the summer solstice, the days gradually shorten, and the sun's altitude gradually lowers. By the autumnal equinox, day and night are again equal, so the weather is the same as in spring. After the autumnal equinox, the days are shorter than the nights, and the sun's altitude is lower, so the layer of atmosphere through which sunlight passes gradually thickens, making the weather gradually colder. By the winter solstice, the days are shortest, the sun's altitude is lowest, and the sunlight passes through the thickest layer of the atmosphere, making the weather the coldest. After the winter solstice, the days gradually lengthen again, and the sun's altitude gradually rises, so the weather gradually warms up. This is the situation of seasonal change.

We have already stated above that the amount of solar heat received in the Northern Hemisphere is greatest at the summer solstice, which should be the hottest time. However, in reality, the summer solstice is not the hottest time; August is the hottest. Also, the amount of solar heat received at the winter solstice is the least, which should be the coldest time, but in reality, the winter solstice is not the coldest; February is the coldest. This phenomenon is called the seasonal lag, which is due to the influence of the atmosphere.

We know that the Earth is surrounded by the atmosphere. Because of the atmosphere, the Earth receives heat from the sun on the one hand, and radiates heat outwards from the surface on the other. We know that the temperature can only increase if the Earth receives more heat from the sun than it radiates from the surface. If the Earth receives less heat than it radiates, the temperature will decrease. Therefore, the summer solstice is the time of year when the Earth receives the most heat, and during this time, the heat received by the Earth's surface is greater than the heat radiated from the surface, so the temperature increases day by day. Thus, from the summer solstice until around August, the temperature continues to increase. When the temperature reaches its maximum, it stops increasing, which is when the amount of heat received is equal to the amount of heat lost. This is the hottest time of the year, so it is not at the summer solstice but around August. The same principle applies in winter, with the lowest temperature reached sometime between January and February. However, climate change is not determined solely by the conditions of one place; it also depends on the relationship with winds and ocean currents from other places. Therefore, the coldest or hottest time of a particular place cannot be determined solely by astronomical theory; it varies considerably from year to year. (The End)

Roosevelt Writes to the American Bankers Association: Very Pleased with Economic Recovery 28

New Orleans: President Roosevelt sent a letter to the American Bankers Association today, which was read by Jesse Jones, Chairman of the Reconstruction Finance Corporation (RFC), at the association's annual meeting. The letter expressed the President's great pleasure with the consolidation of the position of American banks and the great progress in economic recovery in recent years. It stated that the extent of the recovery over the past two years could be seen from bank deposits and collateral, and hoped that all banks would make full use of the new banking laws to provide credit and loans to the business community, industry, and real estate in a stable manner. After Jones read the President's letter, he gave a speech criticizing the methods of interaction between American railroads and banks, stating that the public should give railroads fair access to capital, and that the banking industry's interactions with railroads should be subject to stricter regulations to limit interest rates and other expenses. He said that although the government should immediately stop lending to railroads, the current government loans have lighter interest and therefore the people should spare no effort to make the government not nationalize the railways. Jones briefly described the activities of the RFC, stating that most of the loans borrowed by banks and insurance companies have been repaid, and that the collateral for these loans was not acceptable to ordinary banks, so such rapid repayment was remarkable. (National Telegram, 12th)

New Orleans: Government officials delivered speeches today at the 64th annual meeting of the American Bankers Association, vaguely mentioning the government's plans to withdraw from the banking industry and private business sectors. After the meeting opened, banking leaders spoke first, requesting that the government not interfere in private business. RFC Director Jesse Jones responded, saying that he agreed with the members of the ABA and was eager for the government to withdraw from the lending business as soon as possible, but that such steps should not be taken too hastily. Jones also called for fair treatment of railroads, saying that too many of the country's railroads were controlled by banks, and that banks were making large profits from providing them with financial assistance. Federal Deposit Insurance Corporation (FDIC) Director Crowley stated that banks should make extra efforts to replace government loans with private loans. According to his observation, the reasons why the United States has not been able to have a more stable and efficient banking system in the past are nine: (1) too many undercapitalized banks, (2) inefficient management, (3) unstable operations, (4) excessive loan expansion, (5) excessive competition, (6) lax supervision, (7, 8, and 9) lack of understanding of the social economy and legislative trends related to the banking industry. The ways to remedy this are: (1) replace RFC funds with private funds, (2) effective management, (3) harmonious banking laws, (4) replace bank loans with private loans, (5) avoid the reasons for state government interference, and other major points. ABA President Hieber stated that the public now trusts banks again, saying that the emergency period is gradually passing, and that there are now various reasons why the government should begin to withdraw from the private business sector. Members of the association should strive to work for freedom in a serious and effective process for the development of private business and the creation of industry; otherwise, those who seek to grant greater power to the government and socialize various industries may prevail. The outlook for business is now optimistic, and the Banking Act of 1935 has become a perfect piece of legislation. The RFC Director read President Roosevelt's letter, hoping that bankers would raise commercial credit based on a solid foundation, and said that he was confident that through the cooperation of the banking sector, the business community, and the government, all current problems could soon be resolved. (Reuters, 13th)

(Washington) The Federal Reserve Bank today released a report on rediscount operations, stating that bank loans across the country have increased sharply to help the business community recover. In the week before November 6, member bank loans in 101 cities across the country increased by $1,000,000, mortgage loans increased by $27,000,000, totaling $3,233,000,000, commercial loans increased by $40,000,000, totaling $3,380,000, real estate loans decreased by $4,000,000, totaling $1,142,000,000, and private bonds held by member banks decreased by $82,000,000, totaling $3,084,000,000, but government bonds increased by $59,000,000, totaling $8,236,000,000. A Review of the Philippine Independence Movement (Part 1) 36

— Wu Hanfang

The Philippine Commonwealth government will be established tomorrow. We cannot help but pay great attention to this brand-new independent nation in Asia, because its economy, politics, and culture are all closely related to ours. Now, let us first recount the entire course of its independence movement:

(1) The Beginning of the Independence Movement – After the cessation of armed resistance against the United States, the Filipinos began a peaceful independence movement. However, this movement was previously unorganized. The first political party in the Philippines, the Unionist Party, advocated the permanent merger of the Philippines with the United States, but it had few supporters. Later, the party advocated independence after a period of preparation. At the same time, the Nationalist Party had been established, and they fully advocated independence. In the first election of the Philippine Assembly in 1907, Nationalist Party members held the majority, so the party organized a delegation to strongly advocate for the issue of independence.

For the sake of the independence issue, with the unanimous support of the Philippine Assembly and the support of the former Philippine Governor Taft (former US President), two resident commissioners were selected and sent to Washington. The second commissioner, the current first President of the Commonwealth government, Quezon, was also among them. He served as commissioner from 1909 to 1916, continuously expressing the desire for independence to the US Congress and the American people.

(2) The Policy Adopted by the United States Toward the Philippines – The opinions of general politicians regarding the policy adopted by the United States toward the Philippines were almost the same. That is, the US government would first be in a guiding position, gradually increase their autonomy, and ultimately let them be independent, but it was just a matter of time.

US President McKinley issued an instruction to the Philippine Commission on January 20, 1899, stating his desire that the Philippines would receive the most favorable treatment, incomparable to conquered nations, because the Philippines was not seized from the Filipinos by direct force. We must seek the progress of their culture and education, and the development of their self-governing ability. This responsibility cannot be abandoned.

When President Taft was governor in the Philippines, on December 17, 1903, he said, "American newspapers circulating in the Philippines have consistently advocated the expansion of Filipino administrative power, which means that the Philippines is for the Filipinos." The United States' implementation of various policies in the Philippines is also intended to ensure the phrase "the Philippines is for the Filipinos." For its benefit, evolution, civilization... or independence. The only question now is, what is the best way to bring happiness to the Filipinos? Also, in April 1904, when Taft was Secretary of War, he spoke of the Philippines: "When the Filipinos learn self-government, and gradually increase their experience, we can discuss how to resolve the issue of independence. Or, maintain the status quo, still under the protection of their beloved, selfless, guiding leader, the United States."

In 1908, after the Philippine Assembly was opened, US Governor Roosevelt wrote a letter to the Assembly, saying, "I believe the time for Filipinos to make their own decisions is coming. Do they want to be independent? Or is it better to be under the protection of a strong, selfless force, which can maintain domestic order on the one hand, and prevent foreign invasion on the other?"

President Wilson sent a letter on October 6, 1913, which was forwarded to the Filipinos by Manila Governor Harrison, saying, "We are protectors, not for the benefit of the American people, but for the benefit of the Filipinos. The steps we take are ultimately to give them independence. And prepare them for how they can be independent." On December 2, 1913, he gave another letter to the US Congress, saying, "Their own plans and experiences are naturally better than ours. We must study how to serve them, and think about how to quickly relinquish the responsibility of guardianship."

(3) The Jones Law – The passage of the Jones Law was truly a noteworthy event. Its various plans were all designed for the Philippines to prepare for independence. He introduced this view to both houses of the United States Congress, but it was rejected. However, after final discussion, the Jones Law was passed.

The Jones Law is a resolution declaring the opinion of the American people on the future politics of the Philippines. Its main idea is included in the following narrative.

"Since the American people had no ambition for conquest and expansion of land in the war between the United States and Spain, and the purpose of the American people is always to withdraw their rule in the Philippines, recognize the independence of the Philippine Islands, and allow them to quickly build an autonomous government. Because it is hoped that this purpose will be quickly realized, many political powers are returned to their hands, allowing them to practice themselves, and they will naturally know where responsibility lies, and can complete political independence as soon as possible."

The Jones Law seems like a guarantee given by the American people to the Chinese people. Because what the successive presidents of the United States have stated is only an administrative opinion, which cannot actually bind the United States. In addition, the policy of the US government regarding the ultimate goal of the Philippines is to further expand the power of Filipinos to manage the Philippines. What the Jones Law contributed to the Filipinos was more clear in attitude and more concrete in organization.

The American Provincial Assembly, local public organizations, and various groups all agreed with the Jones Law, and successively passed the Jones Law bill, sincerely willing to be the guarantee of the Jones Law.

In the eyes of the Filipinos, the Jones Law seems like a contract between the American and Filipino people. From the first time they will build an autonomous government, or all the power is in the hands of the Filipinos. Second, American sovereignty cannot be reduced for a while. Third, when the autonomous government is successfully built, prepare to give them complete independence.

(4) The Temporary Suspension of the Independence Movement During the Great War – Not long after the Jones Law was passed, the United States participated in the European Great War. The Filipinos believed that they should not bother the United States at this time, and the argument for the independence movement was temporarily declared terminated.

The Filipinos, according to the orders of the US government, drew out 35,000 people to serve in the European War, and also supplied the United States with several submarines and torpedo destroyers. There were also six thousand sound-minded troops who enlisted in the United States Navy, which can be said to be the Filipinos' slight contribution to the Americans in times of trouble. But the help of the Americans to the Philippine Islands, even in terms of finance alone, can be said to be quite a lot. Americans give 500,000 yuan a year to fund the Philippine Red Cross. Every time the Filipinos raise public bonds, the Americans enthusiastically donate, and the total amount has reached 70 million gold yuan. The Filipinos have achieved a hundred political successes in a short period of time, naturally relying on the help of the United States.

(5) The Revival of the Independence Theory After the War – After the end of the European War, the issue of independence began to be discussed again. On November 7, 1918, the Senate passed a bill to add a committee for the matter of independence. The Independence Committee plans everything to achieve complete separation from the United States. The Senate will adopt any proposals and reports from the Committee as much as possible. The Committee also sent members to the United States to make earnest requests to the United States with gratitude and respect, believing that the Filipinos had done what they should do, and to listen with sympathy, but there was actually no action.

On March 17, 1919, the Philippine Assembly passed the "Declaration of Purpose." This declaration formally describes the status, determination, and importance of the independence issue of the Filipinos. The general idea is that the time has come for us to make a firm decision to discuss the issue of independence. It also repeatedly affirms the expansion of their autonomous powers by the Americans and various generous policies. The Filipinos have always believed and have not changed in the slightest. It also mentions that the Jones Law is a reliable contract. The current state of the Philippine Commonwealth government is very satisfactory to the United States and other countries. The Filipinos have fulfilled what the Americans had hoped for the Filipinos to do in the past, and now the Filipinos are only waiting for the Americans to fulfill their contract.

The representative of the US government in the Philippine Islands has the responsibility to supervise the Filipinos in building the government under the Jones Law. Governor Harrison and the Philippine Senate made a report to the US Congress saying: "I want to state my responsibility as governor, and my opinion is that Filipino self-governing politics is very necessary at present. Presidents Cleveland and McKinley also advocated this. And we know that Mr. Rhodes was elected as the executive by the help of the people, and can maintain order internally and bear international responsibilities externally."

Currency Reform in Tianjin Leads to Sudden Surge in Copper Coin Prices 76

—Prices of Rice and Flour Also Increase—After the Ministry's order to replace cash with banknotes arrived in Tianjin, the local banks and money shops immediately held a meeting the next day and jointly decided to seal up 7.8 million yuan of silver stored in the bank's public treasury. From November 4th, cash redemption was suspended. Tianjin East shops related to Tianjin banks and money shops were directly notified by each exchange firm. In the future, all exchange accounts with the words "cash silver dollar," "silver dollar," "cash yuan," or "yuan" must be changed to the words "national currency." All income and expenditures must comply with the central government's legal tender as valid. Unexpectedly, the resolution of the silver and money shops and the order issued by the Ministry of Finance were exploited by some traitors and merchants to create rumors. From the 5th, the prices of all goods in the city suddenly rose, and the price of copper coins used for change soared from 530 coins per yuan to 500 coins, 480 coins, and at the peak, reached 370 coins. The market price changed several times a day, and commodity prices also increased accordingly. Social rumors spread, and the livelihood of the poor was greatly affected. The tram company operated by a Belgian merchant, which is the main exchange center for copper coins in the city, posts exchange rates every morning. Various exchange businesses also rely on it as a place to operate. However, due to the price increase, they considered it profitable to hoard and monopolize, and arbitrarily set market prices. The number of coins exchanged daily also decreased. On the 9th and 10th, they posted notices in the trams, asking passengers to purchase tickets with silver yuan instead of copper coins, stating that the company would not be responsible for any copper coin market conditions. As a result, disputes frequently arose between passengers and conductors. The Municipal Public Security Bureau issued a notice on November 6th, prohibiting manipulation and monopolies, and prohibiting raising the market prices of rice and flour, but the result was unsuccessful. On November 9th, it convened another meeting of money and grain businesses, ordering them to effectively stabilize prices. Rice and flour must return to the market prices of five days prior. Copper coins were fixed at 500 coins per legal tender yuan. Tram companies were allowed to exchange at 503 coins per yuan, and exchange businesses were allowed to profit three coins after exchanging. At the same time, another strict notice was issued, but on the 10th, due to the official legal price being too high and the difference in the amount received by the shops being too large, they all refused to exchange. Even when purchasing retail goods, if copper coins were needed for change, the shops would rather cancel the transaction than exchange them at the official rate. On the same day, because the tram company had a regular holiday, copper coins were not exchanged to the outside, causing a shortage of cash on the market and making it difficult to turn over. Until the evening, the Municipal Government approved a joint request from the eight district construction offices and issued a strict notice prohibiting hoarding and manipulation, otherwise, they would be punished according to the law. The Public Security Bureau arrested two groups of profiteers hoarding copper coins that evening, and the market price began to stabilize slightly. Until the 11th, the rice and flour businesses followed the official order and effectively suppressed prices. The outflow of copper coins decreased, and the market situation began to stabilize. As for the reason for the rise in copper coin prices, it was mostly due to rampant rumors. Farmers in the surrounding areas did not understand the true nature of legal tender and hoarded copper coins, resulting in an unusual shortage in the city and leading to a surge in prices.

Regarding the issue of shipping silver south from Tianjin, the banking community has held meetings for several days to discuss the matter. If the silver is shipped to the central government, there will be a shortage of cash in the local area, and the money supply will be disrupted. Foreigners will take advantage of this, and the copper coin price increase may still be difficult to avoid. Therefore, Li Da, Governor of the Central Bank, Lu Baimei, Governor of the Bank of China, Zhong Binglu, Manager of the Bank of Communications, Ji Hua, Chairman of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, and Wang Xiaoyan, Chairman of the Money Shop Association, jointly telegraphed to Beijing, requesting that the central government allow them not to ship the silver south and to establish a Tianjin Reserve Custody Committee branch, with Bian Baimei, Governor of the Bank of China in Tianjin, Liu Yushu, Director of the Tianjin Public Security Bureau, Liu Jicheng, Director of the Municipal Finance Bureau, Yang Baoling, Director of the Municipal Public Works Bureau, and Ji Hua, Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, as members responsible for custody. The telegram has been sent, but a reply has not yet been received. (11th)

Suzhou

Investigating Profiteers Buying Hard Currency

After the Ministry of Finance implemented the new currency policy, commodity prices in Suzhou rose sharply at the beginning of implementation, but have recently returned to their original state. Even the price of cigarettes is gradually returning to normal. However, recently, some Zhenjiang cigarette shops in the city have sent staff to urban and rural areas to buy hard currency from shops and residents, offering a premium of 40-50 cash per yuan. It is reported that the hard currency will be secretly transported to Shanghai and sold to a certain place, where a profit of about 20 cents per yuan can be made. The Public Security Bureau has also heard about this and is investigating closely.

Waifeng Money Shop Suddenly Grounded

Jiufeng Money Shop on Guanqian Street, which has been in business for ten years, is considered reputable in the Suzhou money industry. Its deposits and loans each amount to more than 600,000 yuan. On the 12th, there was a sudden run on the bank. The money shop was unprepared and unable to cope, resulting in a standstill. That night, the Money Shop Association convened an emergency meeting to discuss remedies, deciding that the money shop should entrust the Money Shop Association to mortgage some of its fixed assets for cash to maintain operations. Depositors will be paid 30% first, and the remaining payments will be made after the loans are recovered. It is currently open for business and collecting accounts.

Nantong

Joint Defense Patrols in Six Counties of the District

Military police from the six counties of Tong, Ru, Hai, Chong, Qi, and Jing in the Nantong district will begin winter defense operations on the 15th. The district security command has formulated measures to implement joint water and land defense patrols. The county government will also use the Baojia system to investigate and arrest bandits within the territory.

Yangzhou

High Court President Inspects Prison

Zhu Shusheng, President of the Jiangsu High Court, came to Yangzhou for inspection. On the morning of the 10th, accompanied by Luo, President of the Jiangdu District Court, and others, he went to the prison to inspect. The prison warden, Hu Song, presented a register of prisoners. After Zhu glanced through it, he went to inspect the prison. According to the prisoners' request for food relief, Hu, the prison warden, reported that he had been ordered to process prison rehabilitation. It was estimated that 55 prisoners were eligible for parole and had been registered and submitted to the county prison association for review. Only 15 names were approved. Applications for parole for crimes involving robbery, murder, and kidnapping were generally not approved. President Zhu was informed of the situation and immediately summoned Magistrate Ma. However, Ma was in the provincial capital on official business, so Secretary Wang Zhizhi represented him. President Zhu informed him that the government's parole procedures were part of the prison rehabilitation regulations and were not strict. Regardless of the crime, as long as the prisoner showed remorse, he could be paroled according to the law. He instructed him to relay this to Magistrate Ma for handling. It is reported that Zhu crossed south that afternoon after inspecting the prison.

Pinghu

Trial Opens for Murder of Tax Police Case

Gu Yuanfang, captain of the Fourth Detachment of the Tax Police stationed in Hongni Township, was beaten to death by smugglers at midnight on the 14th of last month in the Dai Mutun area while escorting five smugglers. The soldiers Ruan Youcheng and Gu Yuanfang were killed at the same time. The informant reported the incident to the district headquarters, and six suspects were arrested in Jiaxing and sent to the county government for interrogation. On the 12th, the trial judge, Du Shimin, took his seat in the criminal court and brought in the arrested suspects, Liu Shiyuan, Wang Wenyi, Liu Yuqin, Bi Mengqin, Ge Yufu, and Sun Baosheng, and summoned the tax police officer Zhang Yinsong who had made the arrests to testify. As a result, Ge and Sun were found to have no major suspicion and were allowed to be released on bail. The others were returned to custody pending sentencing on the 16th.

Hangzhou

Bank Association Supports Ministry of Finance Currency Policy

The Hangzhou Bank Association passed resolutions at a regular meeting on the afternoon of the 13th: (1) Telegraph the Ministry of Finance to support the government's currency reform policy; (2) Request that issuing reserve branches be established in major commercial ports to strengthen public confidence. The association also sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, instructing various trade associations to change the words "cash silver dollar" and "cash currency" on bills and contracts to "national currency" to ensure uniformity. The Zhong, Zhong, and Jiao banks held a meeting on the 13th to discuss the method of entrusting the 28 branch offices of the Zhejiang Local Bank to exchange legal tender: (1) 1.3 million yuan will be requested from the head office; (2) Counties without branch offices will be entrusted to the post office to exchange legal tender, with the amount depending on the need.

Grand Occasion of Second Group Wedding

The second group wedding in Hangzhou, which had been prepared by the social affairs section of the municipal government for many days, was held at 2 PM on the 12th at the Xihu Auditorium. Sixteen couples participated. They gathered at Jinghu Hall and wore uniforms provided by the municipal government. The municipal government provided cars to send them to the auditorium, which was decorated luxuriously. Approximately 3,000 people attended the ceremony. Led by two pairs of children, the newlyweds entered in single file and bowed. The officiant, Xu Qingfu, the Director of the Finance Department, and Zhou Xiangxian, the Mayor of Hangzhou, gave speeches one after another, saying that group weddings can save expenses, improve customs, and benefit society and the national economy. After the ceremony, the newlyweds returned to Jinghu Hall for refreshments before dispersing.

Ningbo

Progress on the Old Jiang Bridge Project

Since the Old Jiang Bridge in this port was contracted to Shanghai Kangyi Foreign Firm last year to rebuild a steel-concrete bridge, it has been almost a year. The foreign firm previously sent engineer Sike to Ningbo to supervise the workers and expedite the work. The bridge abutment and other projects have been completed one after another, which is quite trustworthy. According to engineer Sike, since the installation of steel bridge beams began last month using a crane, the weather has been clear and the work has been smooth. He is currently speeding up the work and has already begun pouring the cement bridge deck. Recently, if it does not rain or snow and the weather is not too cold, the entire project is expected to be completed on schedule by the end of the year.

Mingguang

Storage Consolidation Deadline Set

The case of storage consolidation in various counties of Anhui Province was originally scheduled to be completed by the end of November. However, current reports show that only five counties are actively progressing, 31 counties are preparing but have not yet made progress, and 25 counties have not yet reported. The provincial government believes that there are few days left until the deadline and cannot tolerate any delays. It has sent another telegram urging them to complete the work on time, otherwise, they will be severely punished. After receiving the telegram, the county government instructed the county storage management committee to comply and expedite the work.

Westbound Encounters 77

— Ji Yuan

Various Aspects of Chongqing (Part 2)

4. Military Villas Scattered Throughout Sichuan In the past, the extortion and plundering by most military personnel in Sichuan Province had almost become a well-known fact throughout the country. One day, this reporter happened to be chatting with someone from Chongqing and learned that there was a so-called "military residence area" outside Tongyuan Gate in Chongqing City. It is normal for military personnel to have residences, but for residences to have an area, and for the so-called residences to have gardens, Western-style houses, pavilions, ball fields, and even zoos, is unique to Chongqing. This reporter, piqued by curiosity, took a car outside Tongyuan Gate to see the situation in the military residence area.

After leaving Tongyuan Gate, looking up from a distance, the uneven Eastern-style Western buildings were clearly visible. The structure of the houses was exquisite and elegant, relying on the mountains and water, surrounded by trees, like a paradise. This reporter, through the introduction of a friend, visited the residence of a certain division commander and saw that all the luxurious equipment in the residence, such as golf courses, indoor tennis courts, exquisite gardens, and cars, were all available. The front pavilion and rear pavilion were arranged exquisitely, and the fragrance of birds and flowers was refreshing. Later, chatting with the tea server in the residence, it was said, "The owner currently has seven wives, and one or two have already separated. In this area, the division commander with the most wives is so-and-so, with more than a dozen. He also has the most money. The owner is always eager to help others, so he not only has no savings but is also heavily in debt." It was also said that "there are no less than a hundred residences in this area, mostly occupied by military personnel above the rank of brigade commander. There are also quite a few who used to be high officials and are now living in leisure." After hearing this, this reporter could not help but be surprised.

After visiting the residence of a certain division commander, I went to visit Chiyuan Garden. It is said that this garden was also a military residence, but now it is rented to a businessman for business. The layout is quite similar to Shanghai's Bansong Garden, but it has hotels and restaurants, dense forests, and a quiet environment, making it a place for wealthy merchants to stay. Many military and political dignitaries hold banquets here.

5. Lifestyle Characteristics: Drinking Tea and Raising Birds The citizens of Chongqing, except for the general coolies, are mostly people of the leisure class. They are content with traditional lifestyles and mostly use tea houses as the only way to pass the time. There are particularly many small tea houses in Chongqing, and the prices are also very cheap. One copper coin can allow you to sit in a tea house for three or four hours, either whispering and gossiping, or shouting loudly and reporting news, or playing chess for recreation, or mediating disputes between others. It is said that in many tea houses in Chongqing, there are members of the Gelaohui organization lurking among them. Sichuanese call Gelaohui "running brother" and call the old man "master." The seniority is the highest, followed by "big brother," "second brother," etc. The discipline in the association is very strict, and there is an obligation to absolutely obey the master. The master has the power of life and death over his subordinates. The Gelaohui ranks are divided into four types: "benevolence, righteousness, propriety, wisdom." Benevolence is the highest, righteousness is the second, propriety is the next, and wisdom is the lower-level organization. It was extremely prosperous during the Taiping Heavenly Kingdom, and its residual power still exists. Many people in rural areas join. If outsiders visit Sichuan Province and can interact with or seek protection from a reasonably reputable member of the Gelaohui, they can be safe wherever they go, otherwise, unfortunate accidents are likely to occur. Recently, I heard that the provincial government has a proposal to restrict the establishment of tea houses.

Raising birds is also one of the lifestyle habits of idle people in Chongqing. They get up early in the morning with nothing to do, so they carry a birdcage and stroll the streets, or wander around parks and forests, sitting sideways and listening to the chirping of birds. This reporter went to Central Park in the morning and, before entering the park gate, heard the sound of birds and the sound of people harmonizing with each other. Even the people of a prosperous age could not surpass this.

6. The Market for Intellectual Laborers In Chongqing, general coolies must go through intermediaries before they can sell their labor or obtain their labor tools, as described above. In addition to this, intellectual laborers also have a place to find work. According to my friend Jiang Jun, in front of Chongqing Central Park, there is a tea house called "Yule," which is a place for middle and primary schools to recruit teachers. If the principal wants to hire a teacher for a certain subject but cannot find one, he can sit idly in the "Yule" tea garden or ask someone to contact the "Yule" tea garden. Unemployed teachers who want to find a suitable job can also go to "Yule" to inquire about news. This kind of organization is quite similar to a job referral agency, but there is no publicly responsible person. It is said that there are quite a few unemployed middle and primary school teachers in Chongqing recently. Wang, the manager of the Chongqing Kaiming Bookstore, told this reporter, "The education situation in Chongqing and nearby counties is very difficult. Schools at all levels have unpaid salaries for more than a year. Ba County once had more than 60 primary schools, but this year it has been reduced to 20. In the past, there was Dongli Middle School in Dongli and Nanli Middle School in Nanli, but now they have been completely cancelled. The source of education funding in Ba County is "Hongzhuang" (the tax levied on the sale of land), meat tax surcharges, fruit donations, and white charcoal donations. The income is not much. Currently, in Ba County alone, there are more than 200 unemployed teachers."

7. Chongqing Municipal Construction Plan On the morning of October 5th, this reporter went to the municipal government to visit Mayor Zhang Biguo. Secretary Zhou Huili received me on his behalf and told me in great detail about the Chongqing municipal construction plan, saying that the current central plan of the municipal government is (1) to control commerce, (2) to guide investment, and (3) to improve production technology, so that annual income continues to increase (before 1932, Chongqing's bristle export income reached 3 million yuan per year, but now it is only 900,000 yuan), (4) The four ministries have established an agricultural guidance center to regulate supply and demand and manage factories to improve the lives of workers, (7) Establish a municipal bank to absorb small capital and provide relief to small merchants, (8) Establish a job referral agency, a small loan office, and a public pawnshop, (9) Establish low-cost restaurants and build low-cost hostels in Chaotianmen, Tongyuanmen, Taipingmen, and other places, (10) Establish a relief home to provide relief to the disabled, elderly, weak, young, infants, and orphans (the current Chongqing relief home can only accommodate 150 people). The above plans are all necessary measures for Chongqing municipal construction and I hope that they can be gradually implemented.

Foreign Exchange Bankers Association Meeting: Silver Deposits Exchanged for Legal Tender 78

British Banks such as Mercantile Bank Agree to Comply, Joint Industrial Associations Request Promulgation of Real Estate Mortgage Regulations

According to the New Voice News Agency, following the Ministry of Finance's announcement that banknotes from the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications would be legal tender, Chinese banks, money shops, and other businesses are complying by exchanging their silver reserves for legal tender. The Shanghai Foreign Exchange Bankers Association held a meeting the afternoon before yesterday at 5:00 PM to discuss the matter. It is reported that British banks and others have agreed to hand over their silver reserves. The Joint Industrial Associations have telegraphed the Ministry of Finance requesting the prompt promulgation of real estate mortgage regulations. Details are as follows:

Chinese Banks and Money Shops Comply

The Shanghai Silver and Money Trades Association, the Shanghai General Chamber of Commerce, various trade associations, and the General Labor Union have all unanimously endorsed the Ministry of Finance's announcement that banknotes from the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications will be legal tender. Simultaneously, all banks, money shops, factories, companies, and businesses are complying by exchanging their silver reserves for legal tender at the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications. Furthermore, the preparatory management committee for issuance is investigating the reserve funds of each issuing bank, and the cash reserves of each bank have been sent to designated warehouses to be stored as issuance reserves. It is reported that preparatory management committees for issuance will be established in various locations.

Foreign Banks Association Convenes Meeting

The Shanghai Foreign Exchange Bankers Association held a meeting at 5:00 PM the afternoon before yesterday at the Mercantile Bank on the Bund. Representatives from twenty banks attended, including Mercantile Bank, HSBC, Standard Chartered Bank, Yokohama Specie Bank, Banque de l'Indochine, Citibank, Hua Bi Bank, Netherlands Trading Society, Bank of Taiwan, Sumitomo Bank, Mitsui Bank, Bank of Chosen, Mitsubishi Bank, Chase Bank, American Express Bank, British Bank, Hua Yi Bank, Wells Fargo, Banque Franco-Chinoise, and Deutsch-Asiatische Bank. The manager of Mercantile Bank presided over the meeting and reported on the letter received from the Central Bank requesting that all banks hand over their silver reserves to be exchanged for legal tender at the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications. A lengthy discussion ensued, and the meeting adjourned around 6:00 PM.

British Banks and Others Agree to Hand Over Silver Reserves

A reporter from the New Voice News Agency learned yesterday from foreign banks that the silver reserves held by various foreign banks in Shanghai, such as Mercantile Bank, HSBC, Citibank, and Yokohama Specie Bank, amounted to 22,220,000 taels and 78,160,000 yuan as of the end of last week. It is reported that British banks such as Mercantile Bank, HSBC, Standard Chartered Bank, and British Bank have all agreed to hand over their silver reserves to be exchanged for legal tender at the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications. It is also reported that American banks such as Citibank, Wells Fargo, Chase Bank, as well as Hua Bi Bank, Deutsch-Asiatische Bank, and Hua Yi Bank have also agreed to comply.

Cash Storage Committees Established in Various Ports

According to the New News Agency, since the Ministry of Finance announced the currency decree, all silver reserves nationwide must be concentrated in the three banks to serve as reserve funds for the issuance of legal tender. It is now learned that the Ministry of Finance, for the convenience of various locations, has decided to establish cash storage committees in major ports across the country. Committee members will be selected from local financial industry leaders and representatives from various sectors. The committee will be subordinate to the preparatory management committee for issuance. In Beiping, the chairman of the Beiping Bankers Association, Zhou Zuomin, will serve on the committee. The implementation in other ports will follow. It is also learned that Zhou Zuomin went to Nanjing on the 12th to meet with Finance Minister Kong to seek instructions. Wu Daquan, the head of the Chinese economic delegation to Japan, has also returned to Tianjin and is currently in Beijing. He is scheduled to visit Shanghai in the coming days.

Joint Industrial Associations Telegraph Support for Legal Tender

The Shanghai Federation of Machine-Made Domestic Goods Factories telegraphed the Ministry of Finance yesterday to express support for legal tender and requested the prompt promulgation of real estate mortgage regulations. The original telegram reads: "To Finance Minister Kong Jun in Nanjing: China's economy has been collapsing in recent years, and agriculture, industry, and commerce are all on the verge of collapse. Your department has taken control, promulgated emergency decrees, nationalized silver, and designated banknotes from the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications as legal tender to prevent the outflow of silver, regulate international exchange rates, establish the country on a foundation of stability, and create a prosperous environment for the market. These are excellent plans that have been praised both domestically and internationally. It is not just our association that sings praises. However, our association is a group of domestic goods industries, and we speak from an industrial perspective. Your department's prudent, thorough, and resolute reforms have already silenced those who spread rumors, but follow-up measures should be implemented as soon as possible. Recently, gold prices have soared, increasing the cost of industrial raw materials imported from abroad. Various prices have also increased directly or indirectly. At a time when people's purchasing power is weak, even if goods are cheap, people cannot afford to buy them. In addition, real estate is sluggish, and funds circulating in the market are decreasing daily. If prices rise while people's purchasing power is weak, the market will not recover. The major plans announced by your department, such as establishing a central reserve bank, increasing the number of real estate mortgage lending banks, promulgating real estate mortgage regulations, and reforming the organization of foreign banks, should be implemented as soon as possible to promote economic recovery and consolidate industry and commerce. Your department has high ambitions and long-term plans, and you have your own strategies, so there is no need for our association to worry excessively. However, even rivers and seas do not reject small streams, so we dare to offer our humble suggestions. We ask for your consideration."

The Signing of the Sino-French Air Transport Agreement 83

Can Be Implemented in Three Months

The Sino-French air transport issue, which has been under discussion for six or seven years, has now been resolved. It has been learned that the Ministry of Transport of the National Government of the Republic of China and the French Ministry of Aviation officially signed the Sino-French air transport agreement a few days ago. The details of the process are as follows:

Negotiation Process

The motive for Sino-French air transport began in 1929 when France was planning an airline from Marseille to Saigon, Vietnam. Under the name of the Eastern Aviation Company, they discussed Sino-French air transport with the Chinese transport authorities to facilitate air transport between the two countries. At that time, some technical issues needed to be confirmed, and a solution could not be reached for a while. Later, the French Far East airline was officially launched, and the need for air transport between China and France and Europe became increasingly apparent. After several rounds of negotiations, the French Minister of Aviation appointed a representative to discuss the matter in earnest. Both sides showed a spirit of cooperation and openness and agreed on a draft. After being approved by the responsible officials, representatives from both sides signed the Sino-French air transport agreement in Nanjing a few days ago.

Main Points of the Agreement

(A) A regular route will be established from Guangzhou via Guangzhou Bay to Hanoi, French Indochina. It will be operated by an airline wholly owned by the Ministry of Transport of the National Government of the Republic of China to carry passengers, goods, and mail back and forth. It will connect with the route of the French airline in Hanoi, French Indochina. (B) The route should be launched within three months after the signing of the agreement. The validity period of the agreement is three years.

Preparation Status

After the agreement was signed, the Ministry of Transport entrusted China National Aviation Corporation to send a plane to test the route from Guangzhou via Guangzhou Bay to Hanoi. At the same time, it prepared a number of pilots to provide service. It is expected that Sino-French air transport will be realized within three months. From then on, air transport between China and France can be linked, which will also enhance the relationship between the two countries.

According to the New News Agency, after the signing of the Sino-French Vietnam Treaty, our Ministry of Foreign Affairs is preparing to establish consulates-general in Hanoi and Saigon in Vietnam to handle the affairs of Chinese merchants and overseas Chinese in Vietnam. After meeting with officials from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs for instructions, he will go to Vietnam to open the consulate on a scheduled date.

General Labor Union Relieves Unemployed Workers 87

Domestic Goods Sales Team Actively Proceeding

The Shanghai General Labor Union believes that Shanghai's industry and commerce are declining, and the number of unemployed workers is increasing daily. As the severe winter is approaching, the fear of life is very pitiful. In addition to submitting a report to the Fifth National Congress requesting that appropriate relief measures be planned, it also organizes a domestic goods sales team for unemployed workers as a temporary relief measure. Since its establishment, the team has been actively carrying out its work, sending people to various domestic goods factories to discuss sales and writing to the Joint Industrial Associations to ask them to collect products for them so that they can promote domestic goods while providing relief to the unemployed. The details are as follows:

Letter to the Joint Industrial Associations

The association wrote to the Federation of Machine-Made Domestic Goods Factories yesterday, saying: "We are writing to inform you that our association, in view of the increasingly serious unemployment problem and the sluggish sales of domestic goods, has established the Shanghai General Labor Union's Domestic Goods Sales Team to employ unemployed workers as team members, undertake the products of various domestic goods factories, distribute them to team members, and sell them inside and outside the city to use the profits to relieve the lives of team members, and to promote domestic goods while providing relief to the unemployed. We have long admired your association's responsibility for leading and supporting various domestic goods factories in Shanghai, and it is the hub for revitalizing national industry. We hope that you will not fail to support our association's modest intentions to relieve unemployment and promote domestic goods, even though the sales force is too small. We are sending you a letter and a copy of the organization rules of the Domestic Goods Sales Team. We would like to ask you to introduce several manufacturers to the team to sell the goods specified by the team, so that both parties can benefit. We hereby inform you in advance and hope for your consideration."

Sending People to Discuss

The association, together with Lu Yinchu and Su Shaotao, the directors of the sales team, sent people to various domestic goods factories to discuss the purchase of goods so that they could be handed over to unemployed workers to sell on their behalf to help them maintain their livelihood. It is reported that those who have completed negotiations include Qiming Cloth Factory, Yixin Toothbrush Factory, Mingxing Toothbrush Factory, Guang Sheng Hang, China Enamel Factory, Jiu Xing Enamel Factory, Hongxing Cloth Factory, Dongya Woolen Factory, and Great China Welfare Rubber Factory. It is reported that negotiations with other factories are continuing.

More Than 100 Trade Associations, Including the Sugar Industry, Request the Abolition of the Bran Tax in Guangdong Province 88

Yesterday, They Jointly Telegraphed to the Fifth National Congress

The Guangdong province's imposition of an additional tax on bran has aroused strong opposition from oil cake manufacturers in various places. In addition to sending representatives to Beijing to petition the Fifth National Congress, more than 100 trade associations in Shanghai, including the sugar industry, have risen up to support them. Yesterday, they jointly telegraphed to the Fifth National Congress requesting its cancellation. The original telegram reads: "To the Fifth National Congress of the Chinese Kuomintang in Nanjing: We have investigated the case of Guangdong province's collection of additional fees on bran, which has caused work stoppages and transportation stoppages among oil cake merchants in various places. Producers, sellers, transporters, and related groups have repeatedly called for its cancellation for more than two months, but it has not been resolved. The harm to the people's livelihood has already been seen in the industry's documents and telegrams, and will not be repeated here. From the perspective of national laws and regulations, since the abolition of likin, except for the import, transit, and export taxes and surtaxes collected by the customs at the time of cargo transportation, and the consolidated tax collected at the time of cargo leaving the factory, there should be no more taxation of goods within the same territory. No matter what the name is, whether it is a tax or a fee, it is prohibited according to the order to abolish likin. Therefore, Article 62 of the Provisional Constitution during the Tutelage Period clearly prohibits disguised likin. The resolution of the National Finance Conference in 1934 regarding the reorganization of local finances listed nine items of unreasonable taxes and fees that should be abolished, including the sixth, which is unfair taxation of the import of goods from other places for the benefit of one place, and the seventh, which is taxes and fees levied on the production or sale of goods. All of these should be abolished by the end of 1934. Those that have not been levied shall not be opened without authorization by any means or in any name. These are all clearly verifiable. From this, it can be seen that Guangdong province's collection of additional fees on bran, no matter what reason it holds or what purpose it serves, is inappropriate in terms of the Provisional Constitution and the political order. It is heard that Guangdong province is vigorously implementing a three-year plan to abolish unreasonable taxes and fees. Now, if what it does is no different from likin and even more no different from unreasonable taxes and fees, it is even more incomprehensible. The reason why likin was abolished and unreasonable taxes and fees were abolished was originally to prevent the development of our country's industry, so we removed the obstacles in order to promote its revitalization. Unexpectedly, Guangdong province has dealt such a heavy blow to the emerging oil cake industry along the Yangtze River. All those who operate domestic industries will be disheartened by this. Our associations deeply sympathize with the suffering of oil cake manufacturers in various places who are unable to bear this harsh tax. Sugar industry, silk industry, cotton cloth industry, paper industry, wood industry, machine dyeing and weaving industry, woolen industry, Western medicine industry, and more than 100 other trade associations in Shanghai."

Shell Explodes on British Warship, Injuring Two 90

Injuries Not Serious

According to the Da Mei Evening News, this morning (the 13th), an empty shell of a ceremonial gun suddenly exploded on the British cruiser HMS Dorsetshire in the Huangpu River. Fish Market Organization Moves Towards Commercialization 91

Limited Number of Positions, Strive for Thrift During Opening, Adopt an Employment System and Increase Worker Welfare

According to the Central News Agency, the preparation of the Shanghai Fish Market of the Ministry of Industry has been reported in previous newspapers. When a reporter met with a certain gentleman from the preparatory committee yesterday and asked about the actual situation of the association, he was assured that the people of the preparatory committee regard this pioneering business as a reform of the fisheries economic system. In addition to finding ways to benefit fishermen, they also drew lessons from the bureaucratization of state-owned enterprises in the past, which often resulted in large organizations, wasted public funds, and various other mistakes. Therefore, the organization of the market this time is striving towards commercialization. The provisional articles of association for the fish market organization have been approved and promulgated by the Ministry of Industry and the Executive Yuan. In addition to the board of directors and supervisors, it is stipulated that there will be three sections, with a total of only 20 staff members. The Ministry of Industry also ordered that thrift be practiced during the opening and that the fixed number of personnel should not be fully employed. The monthly expenses are only set at 3,000 yuan, which will be filled by the preparatory personnel. There will be no additions until the business develops in the future, and then expansion will be carried out. As for the dock workers, the Ministry of Industry has formulated an outline of the management rules for loading and unloading workers of directly-administered state-owned enterprises, and the ministry will send personnel to be in charge of these affairs to thoroughly break the contracting system and increase worker welfare.

Disaster Relief is Saving Lives; Donate Just One More Copper Coin, Save One More Life

Chinese and Foreign Relief Association Reports on the Drought in Anhui Province 97

The Chinese and Foreign Relief Association on Renji Road, previously reported that various legal entities in Yingshang County, Anhui Province, sent representatives to Shanghai to beg for relief due to the severe drought. Their report on the disaster situation was published in previous newspapers and attracted attention. However, few people know that the drought is rampant in Anhui Province, not just in Yingshang County. Now, the association has also received representatives from Fuyang, Linquan, Taihe, Fengtai, and other counties, or received letters from them, all stating that the drought is severe and the situation is tragic. The various reports are excerpted as follows: A letter from various legal entities in Fuyang states that since the summer, the three hottest periods have been without rain. Sorghum, beans, and taros have withered. By the Mid-Autumn Festival, the heat was more intense than in mid-summer, causing the replanting of miscellaneous grains to completely dry up. Now that it is late autumn, farmers are mostly impoverished. With all means exhausted, extending to the severe winter and spring, they will inevitably starve to death on the roads and fill the ditches. Special representatives were sent to personally present the catastrophic situation, begging for investigation and relief. A letter from various legal entities in Taihe County states that since the summer, the drought has been rampant, with no rain for months, bare land everywhere, and springs drying up at the bottom of wells, resulting in no harvest of crops. Famine is imminent, and the prospects are bleak. The four borders are desolate, and the land is barren. It is a drought that has not been seen in decades. As winter approaches, people will cry from hunger and cold, and they fear they will die in ditches. Currently, there are starving people everywhere, and relief is urgently needed. Please quickly allocate funds for relief. A letter from County Magistrate Xiang of Fengtai County reports that since the summer, no rain has fallen in June, July, and August, the fields have cracked, and the ditches have dried up, resulting in an unprecedented drought. Almost no crops have been harvested in all 94 villages in the county. Vast fields are barren, and it is a desolate sight everywhere. Now that it is just early winter, tree leaves and grass roots have been almost completely collected. People are fleeing on the roads, and famine is rampant. It is estimated that more than 100,000 people are in urgent need of relief. Please quickly allocate relief funds to save the dying victims.

Statement by the China International Famine Relief Commission: No Joint Fundraising 98

Since its establishment in 1921, the China International Famine Relief Commission has established branches in 13 provinces. In Jiangsu Province, only a Shanghai office is located at 505 Henan Road, Shanghai. The newly established fundraising section is attached to the Shanghai office. In the past years, it has handled emergency accounts for major floods and droughts and disaster prevention projects, raising donations through proper methods. This time, the Jianghe flood account was approved and filed by the Ministry of Political Affairs, and the receipts were stamped with the Ministry's seal to show caution. Since fundraising began in August, it has received enthusiastic support from people at home and abroad. However, recently, people have often questioned the issue of joint fundraising and have even criticized it on the phone, saying that donating thirty cents of foreign currency will bring a hope of 1,500 yuan, which is close to enticement and similar to gambling. The commission has heard about these things every day and is greatly troubled. Therefore, it solemnly declares that there is absolutely no such thing as joint fundraising. Please disclose this to avoid misunderstandings from the outside world.

Within the Area of ​​Road Construction Beyond the Boundary in West Shanghai: Residents Can Connect to Electricity Without Difficulty; No Need to Submit the Shanghai Municipal Council Donation Ticket for Verification

The electricity supply issue in the area of ​​road construction beyond the boundary in West Shanghai has been resolved since the Municipal Government and the West Shanghai Power Company signed a contract on January 4 this year. After that, all users in the area can directly apply to the company for electricity connection without difficulty. Recently, it was heard that when electrical material stores undertaking the installation of electrical equipment for users in the area apply to the company for electricity connection on behalf of the users, they claim to the users that they must show the Shanghai Municipal Council patrolmen's donation receipt to the company before they can be allowed to connect to electricity. After inquiring with the person in charge, this is not true. The area completely belongs to the Chinese territory, and the West Shanghai Power Company is a company specially authorized by the Municipal Government to operate electrical business in the area. There is absolutely no reason to ask users for the Shanghai Municipal Council's donation receipt.
